</span><span class="cl-a1c951e4">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-a1c9aa68"><p class="cl-a1c95e1e"><span class="cl-a1c951e4">449.43</span></p></td><td Summit, the two countries continued their negotiations that led to a peace deal.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1c9aa5e"><p class="cl-a1c95e1e"><span class="cl-a1c951f8">Chad</span><span forbade the presence of rebel elements in both countries.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1c9aa5e"><p class="cl-a1c95e1e"><span class="cl-a1c951e4">No</span><span class="cl-a1c951e4"> </span><span class="cl-a1c95e1e"><span class="cl-a1c951e4">No</span><span class="cl-a1c951e4"> </span><span class="cl-a1c951e4">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td direction, the peace deal left the resumption of diplomatic relations between the two countries to the appreciation of the two heads of state who were not present at the signing of the agreement.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1c9aa5e"><p class="cl-a1c95e1e"><span class="cl-a1c951e4">No</span><span class="cl-a1c951e4"> </span><span class="cl-a1c951e4">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr countries.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1c9aa72"><p class="cl-a1c95e1e"><span class="cl-a1c951e4">No</span><span class="cl-a1c951e4"> </span><span class="cl-a1c951e4">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr ceremony.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1c9aa5e"><p class="cl-a1c95e1e"><span class="cl-a1c951f8">Libya</span><span class="cl-a1c951e4"> </span><span class="cl-a1c951e4">initiated</span><span North Korean officials met directly and held bilateral negotiations.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1d5264a"><p class="cl-a1d4cd6c"><span class="cl-a1d4c114">United</span><span class="cl-a1d4c114"> agreement proceeded smoothly with two key exceptions.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1d5264a"><p class="cl-a1d4cd6c"><span class="cl-a1d4c10a">No</span><span class="cl-a1d4c10a"> </span><span progress.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1d5262c"><p class="cl-a1d4cd6c"><span class="cl-a1d4c10a">No</span><span class="cl-a1d4c10a"> </span><span class="cl-a1d4c10a">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr Lebanon and the ground war continued on 12 and 13 August with renewed intensity.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1e0f9de"><p class="cl-a1e0b2a8"><span class="cl-a1e0a6be">Israel</span><span </span><span class="cl-a1e0a6b4">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-a1e0f9ea"><p class="cl-a1e0b2a8"><span class="cl-a1e0a6b4">451.44</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f979c8">Libya</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979be">initiated</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979c8">mediation</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979be">toward</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979c8">Sudan;Chad</span><span class="cl-a1f979be">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-a1f9c45a"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">453.43</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c450"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">Eritrea joined the effort as well, and the two sides met with both mediators that same day.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c450"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979c8">Eritrea</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979be">initiated</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979c8">mediation;meeting</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979be">toward</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979c8">Sudan;Chad</span><span class="cl-a1f979be">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-a1f9c45c"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">453.44</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c45b"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">This activity was situated within a larger mediation effort that began on February 21, 2007, when a series of regular meetings involving ministers from Chad, Sudan, Libya, and Eritrea were initiated.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c45b"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">No</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979be">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-a1f9c45a"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">453.45</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c450"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">These meetings were aimed at defusing border tensions between Chad and Sudan and getting them to both normalize relations and implement the February 2006 Tripoli Agreement that ended the Chad-Sudan I crisis.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c450"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">No</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979be">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-a1f9c45c"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">453.46</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c45b"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">As part of this effort, a contingency of Libyan, Eritrean, Sudanese, and Chadian military and security observers was deployed in the border region between Chad and Sudan in March 2007 in order to report on and ultimately prevent border incursions and other incidents.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c45b"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">No</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979be">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-a1f9c45a"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">453.47</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c450"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">The observer mission was part of the Tripoli Agreement signed the previous year but had only recently been deployed as the two sides had come under increasingly intense pressure to implement the agreement and accept UN peacekeepers in the border region.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c450"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">No</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979be">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-a1f9c45c"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">453.48</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c45b"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">Libya had been putting pressure on both sides to resist the international efforts to get UN peacekeepers on the ground, preferring instead a regional alternative to lessen the need for UN troops.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c45b"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">No</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979be">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-a1f9c45a"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">453.49</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c450"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">Triki delivered a plan drafted by al-Gaddafi that was intended to get the two sides to return to the negotiating table, resolve the situation peacefully, ease their tensions, and implement the Tripoli Agreement.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c450"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">No</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979be">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-a1f9c45c"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">453.50</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c45b"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">On April 10, Chad apologizes for the previous day's border incident.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c45b"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">No</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979be">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-a1f9c45a"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">453.51</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c450"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">The following day, both sides began toning down their threats and said they were looking to resolve the situation peacefully and improve relations with each other.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c450"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">No</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979be">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-a1f9c45c"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">453.52</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c45b"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">However, Sudan said that the Chadian apology is not sufficient and that it required more guarantees from Chad that future aggression would not occur.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c45b"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">No</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979be">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-a1f9c45a"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">453.53</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c450"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">On April 12, Libya and Eritrea dispatched additional military and security observers to the border region between Chad and Sudan in response to the recent hostilities.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c450"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979c8">Libya;Eritrea</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979be">initiated</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979c8">deployment</span><span class="cl-a1f979c8"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979c8">to</span><span class="cl-a1f979c8"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979c8">area</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-a1f9c45c"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">453.54</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c45b"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">Two days later, Chad said it would continue to use military force if Chadian rebels and pro-Sudanese militias cross into Chadian territory, and that it hoped Sudan would allow it the right of pursuit in the event that said actors crossed back into Sudanese territory after attacking.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c45b"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">NA</span><span class="cl-a1f979be"> </span><span class="cl-a1f979be">No</span><span class="cl-a1f979be">453.55</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c464"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">On April 16 and 17, Libya, Eritrea, and the Community of Sahel and Saharan States and size and of the AU peacekeeping force deployed to deal with the conflict in Darfur, Sudan.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a1f9c464"><p class="cl-a1f984ea"><span class="cl-a1f979be">No</span><span and Ethiopia shifted its troop positions in response.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a202fae9"><p class="cl-a202caf0"><span class="cl-a202bff6">Ethiopia</span><span class="cl-a202bfec"> </span><span class="cl-a202fae8"><p class="cl-a202caf0"><span class="cl-a202bfec">On September 25, Ethiopia sent a formal letter to Eritrea threatening to terminate the Algiers Agreement unless Eritrea began complying with said agreement.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a202fae8"><p class="cl-a202caf0"><span class="cl-a202bff6">Ethiopia</span><span class="cl-a202bfec"> </span><span of diplomatic relations and resumption of cooperation between the two countries, as well as the establishment of a tripartite summit to oversee their previous agreements that was to be sponsored by class="cl-a244a06a"> </span><span class="cl-a244a07e">end</span><span class="cl-a244a07e"> </span><span class="cl-a244a07e">of</span><span class="cl-a244a07e"> </span><span class="cl-a244a07e">crisis</span><span class="cl-a244a06a">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-a244e0fd"><p class="cl-a244abc8"><span class="cl-a244a06a">461.35</span></p></td><td class="cl-a244e0fc"><p class="cl-a244abc8"><span class="cl-a244a06a">The US and China were both involved in the crisis.</span></p></td><td class="cl-a244e0fc"><p class="cl-a244abc8"><span class="cl-a244a06a">No</span><span class="cl-a244a06a"> </span><span class="cl-a244a06a">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr the joint US-South Korean military exercises, but its main involvement was effectively resisting US calls for a tougher line against North Korea throughout the crisis.</span></p></td><td
